Hi Jason- this is a good start and the most recent month of invoicing for each is needed along with a copy of the respective service agreements or contracts in place. The process takes about 30 days, so we’d be set up on or about Aug 1. 

 

Once I have those, I’ll loop you in with the WM team to begin the onboarding and ensure things go smoothly. If there are other waste related vendors (bulk removal, equipment rental, etc) that you want to include on the centralized invoice, please send the recent invoicing along as well.  To clarify, it’s a $25/mo fee. 

 

Thanks much,

Jeff

## Email Content

Hi Jason- this is a good start and the most recent month of invoicing for each is needed along with a copy of the respective service agreements or contracts in place. The process takes about 30 days, so we’d be set up on or about Aug 1. 

 

Once I have those, I’ll loop you in with the WM team to begin the onboarding and ensure things go smoothly. If there are other waste related vendors (bulk removal, equipment rental, etc) that you want to include on the centralized invoice, please send the recent invoicing along as well.  To clarify, it’s a $25/mo fee. 

 

Thanks much,

Jeff

Hello,

 

We received a repair request for the following locations compactor. It appears this unit is client owned. We can send someone out for the compactor repair, but we will need a $1,500 NTE (Not-to-Exceed) approved.

 

If WMCS sends a repair tech to repair property-owned equipment, we need to get a preapproved NTE of $1,500. This $1,500 covers the cost of the first trip to send the tech to the property as well as any repairs the tech can make during that trip if costs are less than $1,500. For additional repairs, a quote will be prepared and presented for the property to approve before proceeding. Whether or not the property decides to move forward with the quoted repairs, the first trip charge will be billed up to, but not exceeding, $1,500 (unless otherwise told in advance).

 

Please let us know if this is approved.

 

 

 

 

Thank you,

 

Jessica Shrader

Hi Christina,

 

I have requested that our repair team provide you with an update on the repairs.  

 

The compactor rental is $519.16.

 

We do not provide credit on rentals when a compactor is down.  It would be similar to a leased vehicle breaking down and being put in the shop, you would still have to pay your monthly lease while it is in the shop.

 

WM is discounting the opentop.  That is also not a common practice, or required by our contract, but something we do as a courtesy to Greystar.

Hi Christina,

 

I have requested that our repair team provide you with an update on the repairs.  

 

The compactor rental is $519.16.

 

We do not provide credit on rentals when a compactor is down.  It would be similar to a leased vehicle breaking down and being put in the shop, you would still have to pay your monthly lease while it is in the shop.

 

WM is discounting the opentop.  That is also not a common practice, or required by our contract, but something we do as a courtesy to Greystar.

 

Thanks,

Hi Christina,

 

I have requested that our repair team provide you with an update on the repairs.  

 

The compactor rental is $519.16.

 

We do not provide credit on rentals when a compactor is down.  It would be similar to a leased vehicle breaking down and being put in the shop, you would still have to pay your monthly lease while it is in the shop.

 

WM is discounting the opentop.  That is also not a common practice, or required by our contract, but something we do as a courtesy to Greystar.

I have requested that our repair team provide you with an update on the repairs.  

 

The compactor rental is $519.16.

 

We do not provide credit on rentals when a compactor is down.  It would be similar to a leased vehicle breaking down and being put in the shop, you would still have to pay your monthly lease while it is in the shop.

 

WM is discounting the opentop.  That is also not a common practice, or required by our contract, but something we do as a courtesy to Greystar.

Hi Christina,

 

I have requested that our repair team provide you with an update on the repairs.  

 

The compactor rental is $519.16.

 

We do not provide credit on rentals when a compactor is down.  It would be similar to a leased vehicle breaking down and being put in the shop, you would still have to pay your monthly lease while it is in the shop.

 

WM is discounting the opentop.  That is also not a common practice, or required by our contract, but something we do as a courtesy to Greystar.

Hi Christina,

 

I have requested that our repair team provide you with an update on the repairs.  

 

The compactor rental is $519.16.

 

We do not provide credit on rentals when a compactor is down.  It would be similar to a leased vehicle breaking down and being put in the shop, you would still have to pay your monthly lease while it is in the shop.

 

WM is discounting the opentop.  That is also not a common practice, or required by our contract, but something we do as a courtesy to Greystar.

 

Thanks,

Hi Christina,

 

I have requested that our repair team provide you with an update on the repairs.  

 

The compactor rental is $519.16.

 

We do not provide credit on rentals when a compactor is down.  It would be similar to a leased vehicle breaking down and being put in the shop, you would still have to pay your monthly lease while it is in the shop.

 

WM is discounting the opentop.  That is also not a common practice, or required by our contract, but something we do as a courtesy to Greystar.

Hi Christina,

 

I have requested that our repair team provide you with an update on the repairs.  

 

The compactor rental is $519.16.

 

We do not provide credit on rentals when a compactor is down.  It would be similar to a leased vehicle breaking down and being put in the shop, you would still have to pay your monthly lease while it is in the shop.

 

WM is discounting the opentop.  That is also not a common practice, or required by our contract, but something we do as a courtesy to Greystar.

Hi Christina,

 

I have requested that our repair team provide you with an update on the repairs.  

 

The compactor rental is $519.16.

 

We do not provide credit on rentals when a compactor is down.  It would be similar to a leased vehicle breaking down and being put in the shop, you would still have to pay your monthly lease while it is in the shop.

 

WM is discounting the opentop.  That is also not a common practice, or required by our contract, but something we do as a courtesy to Greystar.

Morning Jeff,

 

Has Christina conveyed why she believes WM is not working with them on this matter?

 

Just some food for thought…

 

The property reported the compactor down on 6/4.  The tech was onsite with 24 hours, and the original reported matter was resolved (it wasn’t compacting).  From what I understand, staff also noted there was an issue with the rollers.  Local Ops let the repair team know on 6/5 that the compactor needed to be brought in to the shop in order to fix that specific issue.  The compactor was picked up on 6/9 and last note from the shop was that it should be repaired early next week.  The ETA on the return of the equipment was communicated to the Property Manager on 6/10 – so one day after the compactor was removed.

 

A temporary OT was delivered on 6/6.  The local division was actually cutoff for deliveries until 6/10, but Team Greystar was able to push the urgency and get it delivered before the weekend.  The typical cost for a temp 30Y OT in this area would be $75.00 delivery, $450.00 haul, $71.90 disposal/ton, $90.00 monthly rental.  With Greystar, even though we are not contractually obligated, we discount the costs when this property’s WM compactor equipment is down to $0.00 delivery, $125.00 haul, $71.90 disposal/ton, $0.00 monthly rental.  

 

Rebekah is taking a much-deserved day off, but I’m sure she’ll chime in further on Monday.  If we can get some insight on what the specific concern is, so that we are better able to respond, it would be appreciated.

Hi Christina,

 

I have requested that our repair team provide you with an update on the repairs.  

 

The compactor rental is $519.16.

 

We do not provide credit on rentals when a compactor is down.  It would be similar to a leased vehicle breaking down and being put in the shop, you would still have to pay your monthly lease while it is in the shop.

 

WM is discounting the opentop.  That is also not a common practice, or required by our contract, but something we do as a courtesy to Greystar.

 

Thanks,

I wanted to reach out because we are trying to figure out what GL Codes are being used to calculate Mighty 90 compliance?[Jessica Reznik]   There are a number of GL Codes, which are listed, but there are other components to the score that factor in.  GL codes are a good guide for compliance, but the focus should be on the compliant supplier in the category, not the GL code. 

 

I saw the list on power BI, but the list is not all conclusive. For instance, I do not see appliances and all of the trash GLs.[Jessica Reznik]  Correct.  Please see comment above.

 

We also have some properties that have bulk trash expenses, and we need to know what GLs we can use that will not count towards compliance. [Jessica Reznik] Bulk trash is included in Mighty 90’s.  Please see the list of compliant supplier to ensure that you are receiving Best In Class pricing from our bulk suppliers. 

 

How do we get mighty 90s compliance updated? Moderno is located in New Braunfels and can only use NBU for trash, and it is showing at 0% on the KPI dashboard instead of being listed as blank.[Jessica Reznik]  Looping in @Advantage Waste Solutions <mailto:waste@greystar.com>  to look into this.  This can also be cured by getting setup on the WM National Billing Program for $25 per month.  That will switch the billing to WM, and allow us to see your sites waste data, populate client waste data reporting, and review your site for optimization opportunities.  it also allows WM to support your property with future requests and handle daily service request through our national account team at WM.

 

I also have a property, Allora Alamo Heights, that is using Waste Management but is showing as non-compliant because Conservice is paying the waste management bill. Can you advise?[Jessica Reznik]   This is something that we are working on, but I would recommend considering moving to the National Account.  If you are going through Conservice with Waste Management, that means you are on a local account and not rolled into the national account.  I'll second what Jessica shared here.  We can get that started with just your approval.  It means the property will get moved over to Consolidated Billing through Greystar and the site will not pay Conservice anymore.  However, all other things remain constant.  Its just changing the billing address for the most part.
